{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_9ed8eb8c72ab422982a74ba2","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t//! Scoped Meilisearch key rotation (plan §13.21).\n2\t//!\n3\t//! Implements the leader-based rotation sequence:\n4\t//! 1. Mint new scoped key via Meilisearch `POST /keys`\n5\t//! 2. Write new generation to Redis hash\n6\t//! 3. Wait for all live pods to observe new generation (beacon check)\n7\t//! 4. Drain wait for stragglers\n8\t//! 5. `DELETE /keys/{previous_uid}` on all Meilisearch nodes\n9\t//! 6. Clear previous from Redis hash\n10\t\n11\tuse miroir_core::config::MiroirConfig;\n12\tuse miroir_core::task_store::{RedisTaskStore, SearchUiScopedKey, TaskStore};\n13\tuse std::sync::Arc;\n14\tuse std::time::Duration;\n15\tuse tracing::{info, warn, error};\n16\t\n17\tuse crate::routes::indexes::MeilisearchClient;\n18\t\n19\t/// State for the scoped key rotation background task.\n20\t#[derive(Clone)]\n21\tpub struct ScopedKeyRotationState {\n22\t    pub config: Arc<MiroirConfig>,\n23\t    pub redis: RedisTaskStore,\n24\t    pub pod_id: String,\n25\t}\n26\t\n27\t/// Response body for the manual rotation endpoint.\n28\t#[derive(serde::Serialize)]\n29\tpub struct RotateScopedKeyResponse {\n30\t    pub status: String,\n31\t    pub index_uid: String,\n32\t    pub generation: i64,\n33\t    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n34\t    pub previous_uid_revoked: Option<String>,\n35\t    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n36\t    pub error: Option<String>,\n37\t}\n38\t\n39\t/// Request body for the manual rotation endpoint.\n40\t#[derive(serde::Deserialize)]\n41\tpub struct RotateScopedKeyRequest {\n42\t    /// If true, bypass the timing gate and rotate immediately.\n43\t    #[serde(default)]\n44\t    pub force: bool,\n45\t}\n46\t\n47\t/// Run the background scoped key rotation loop.\n48\tpub async fn run_scoped_key_rotator(state: ScopedKeyRotationState) {\n49\t    if !state.config.search_ui.enabled {\n50\t        return;\n51\t    }\n52\t\n53\t    let check_interval = Duration::from_secs(3600); // Check every hour\n54\t    let mut interval = tokio::time::interval(check_interval);\n55\t\n56\t    info!(\"scoped key rotation background task started\");\n57\t\n58\t    loop {\n59\t        interval.tick().await;\n60\t\n61\t        // Refresh our own pod presence heartbeat\n62\t        if let Err(e) = state.redis.register_pod_presence(&state.pod_id) {\n63\t            warn!(pod_id = %state.pod_id, error = %e, \"failed to register pod presence\");\n64\t        }\n65\t\n66\t        // Try to acquire the rotation leader lease\n67\t        let lease_scope = \"search_ui_key_rotation\";\n68\t        let lease_now = now_ms();\n69\t        let lease_ttl_ms = (state.config.leader_election.lease_ttl_s as i64) * 1000;\n70\t        let expires_at = lease_now + lease_ttl_ms;\n71\t\n72\t        match state.redis.try_acquire_leader_lease(lease_scope, &state.pod_id, expires_at, lease_now) {\n73\t            Ok(true) => {}\n74\t            Ok(false) => continue, // Another pod holds the lease\n75\t            Err(e) => {\n76\t                warn!(error = %e, \"failed to acquire rotation leader lease\");\n77\t                continue;\n78\t            }\n79\t        }\n80\t\n81\t        // We are the leader — check each index for rotation need\n82\t        let indexes = discover_scoped_indexes(&state).await;\n83\t        for index_uid in indexes {\n84\t            if let Err(e) = check_and_rotate(&state, &index_uid, false).await {\n85\t                error!(index = %index_uid, error = %e, \"scoped key rotation failed\");\n86\t            }\n87\t        }\n88\t\n89\t        // Renew the lease\n90\t        let _ = state.redis.renew_leader_lease(\n91\t            lease_scope,\n92\t            &state.pod_id,\n93\t            now_ms() + lease_ttl_ms,\n94\t        );\n95\t    }\n96\t}\n97\t\n98\t/// Check if a scoped key needs rotation and perform it if so.\n99\tpub async fn check_and_rotate(\n100\t    state: &ScopedKeyRotationState,\n101\t    index_uid: &str,\n102\t    force: bool,\n103\t) -> Result<RotateScopedKeyResponse, String> {\n104\t    let current = state.redis.get_search_ui_scoped_key(index_uid)\n105\t        .map_err(|e| format!(\"redis read failed: {e}\"))?;\n106\t\n107\t    // Timing gate check (skip if force)\n108\t    if !force {\n109\t        if !should_rotate(&current, &state.config) {\n110\t            return Ok(RotateScopedKeyResponse {\n111\t                status: \"skipped\".into(),\n112\t                index_uid: index_uid.into(),\n113\t                generation: current.as_ref().map(|k| k.generation).unwrap_or(0),\n114\t                previous_uid_revoked: None,\n115\t                error: None,\n116\t            });\n117\t        }\n118\t    }\n119\t\n120\t    // Step 1: Mint new scoped key via Meilisearch POST /keys\n121\t    let client = MeilisearchClient::new(state.config.node_master_key.clone());\n122\t    let (new_key, new_uid) = mint_scoped_key(&client, &state.config, index_uid).await?;\n123\t\n124\t    // Step 2: Write new generation to Redis\n125\t    let new_generation = current.as_ref().map(|k| k.generation + 1).unwrap_or(1);\n126\t    let previous_uid = current.as_ref().map(|k| k.primary_uid.clone());\n127\t    let previous_key = current.as_ref().map(|k| k.primary_key.clone());\n128\t\n129\t    let scoped_key = SearchUiScopedKey {\n130\t        index_uid: index_uid.into(),\n131\t        primary_key: new_key.clone(),\n132\t        primary_uid: new_uid.clone(),\n133\t        previous_key,\n134\t        previous_uid: previous_uid.clone(),\n135\t        rotated_at: now_ms(),\n136\t        generation: new_generation,\n137\t    };\n138\t\n139\t    state.redis.set_search_ui_scoped_key(&scoped_key)\n140\t        .map_err(|e| format!(\"redis write failed: {e}\"))?;\n141\t\n142\t    info!(\n143\t        index = %index_uid,\n144\t        generation = new_generation,\n145\t        \"new scoped key minted, waiting for pod observation\"\n146\t    );\n147\t\n148\t    // Step 3: Observe our own beacon immediately\n149\t    state.redis.observe_search_ui_scoped_key(\n150\t        &state.pod_id,\n151\t        index_uid,\n152\t        new_generation,\n153\t    ).map_err(|e| format!(\"beacon write failed: {e}\"))?;\n154\t\n155\t    // Step 4: Wait for drain period and check beacons\n156\t    let drain_s = state.config.search_ui.scoped_key_rotation_drain_s;\n157\t    let drain_deadline = tokio::time::Instant::now() + Duration::from_secs(drain_s);\n158\t\n159\t    let mut previous_revoked: Option<String> = None;\n160\t\n161\t    loop {\n162\t        // Get live pods\n163\t        let live_pods = state.redis.get_live_pods()\n164\t            .map_err(|e| format!(\"get_live_pods failed: {e}\"))?;\n165\t\n166\t        // Check if all live pods have observed the new generation\n167\t        let (all_observed, unobserved) = state.redis.check_scoped_key_observation(\n168\t            index_uid,\n169\t            new_generation,\n170\t            &live_pods,\n171\t        ).map_err(|e| format!(\"beacon check failed: {e}\"))?;\n172\t\n173\t        if all_observed {\n174\t            info!(\n175\t                index = %index_uid,\n176\t                generation = new_generation,\n177\t                \"all live pods observed new generation, revoking previous key\"\n178\t            );\n179\t\n180\t            // Step 6: Delete previous key from Meilisearch and }\n225\t\n226\t        // Wait before rechecking (every 10 seconds)\n227\t        tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_secs(10)).await;\n228\t    }\n229\t}\n230\t\n231\t/// Check if rotation should backoff_start_minutes: u64,\n166\t        backoff_max_hours: u64,\n167\t    ) -> (bool, Option<u64>) {\n168\t        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n169\t        let now = now_ms();\n170\t        let state = inner.state.entry(ip.to_string()).or_default();\n171\t\n172\t        // Check if we're in backoff mode\n173\t        if let Some(backoff_until) = state.backoff_until_ms {\n174\t            if backoff_until > now {\n175\t                let wait_seconds = ((backoff_until - now) / 1000) as u64;\n176\t                return (false, Some(wait_seconds));\n177\t            }\n178\t            // Backoff expired, clear it\n179\t            state.backoff_until_ms = None;\n180\t        }\n181\t\n182\t        // Clean old timestamps outside the window\n183\t        state.request_timestamps_ms.retain(|&ts| now - ts < window_ms as i64);\n184\t\n185\t        // Check if limit exceeded\n186\t        if state.request_timestamps_ms.len() >= limit as usize {\n187\t            // Enter backoff mode after threshold consecutive failures\n188\t            let failed = state.failed_count + 1;\n189\t            state.failed_count = failed;\n190\t\n191\t            if failed >= failed_threshold {\n192\t                let backoff_minutes = backoff_start_minutes * (1u64 << ((failed - failed_threshold) as u64).min(7)); // Cap at 2^7 = 128x\n193\t                let backoff_seconds = (backoff_minutes * 60).min(backoff_max_hours * 3600);\n194\t                state.backoff_until_ms = Some(now + (backoff_seconds as i64 * 1000));\n195\t                return (false, Some(backoff_seconds));\n196\t            }\n197\t\n198\t            return (false, None);\n199\t        }\n200\t\n201\t        // Record this request\n202\t        state.request_timestamps_ms.push(now);\n203\t        (true, None)\n204\t    }\n205\t\n206\t    /// Reset rate limit and backoff state on successful login.\n207\t    pub fn reset(&self, ip: &str) {\n208\t        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n209\t        inner.state.remove(ip);\n210\t    }\n211\t\n212\t    /// Record a failed login attempt (for backoff calculation).\n213\t    pub fn record_failure(&self, ip: &str, failed_threshold: u32, backoff_start_minutes: u64, backoff_max_hours: u64) -> Option<u64> {\n214\t        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n215\t        let now = now_ms();\n216\t        let state = inner.state.entry(ip.to_string()).or_default();\n217\t\n218\t        state.failed_count += 1;\n219\t\n220\t        if state.failed_count >= failed_threshold {\n221\t            let backoff_minutes = backoff_start_minutes * (1u64 << ((state.failed_count - failed_threshold) as u64).min(7));\n222\t            let backoff_seconds = (backoff_minutes * 60).min(backoff_max_hours * 3600);\n223\t            state.backoff_until_ms = Some(now + (backoff_seconds as i64 * 1000));\n224\t            return Some(backoff_seconds);\n225\t        }\n226\t\n227\t        None\n228\t    }\n229\t}\n230\t\n231\timpl Default for LocalAdminRateLimiter {\n232\t    fn default() -> Self {\n233\t        Self::new()\n234\t    }\n235\t}\n236\t\n237\t/// Get current time in milliseconds since Unix epoch.\n238\tfn now_ms() -> i64 {\n239\t    std::time::SystemTime::now()\n240\t        .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)\n241\t        .unwrap_or_default()\n242\t        .as_millis() as i64\n243\t}\n244\t\n245\t/// Shared application state for admin }\n334\t}\n335\t\n336\t/// Response for GET /_miroir/topology (plan §10 JSON shape).\n337\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n338\tpub struct TopologyResponse {\n339\t    pub shards: Err(format!(\"invalid rate limit format: '{}', expected 'N/UNIT'\", s));\n529\t    }\n530\t    let limit: u64 = parts[0].parse()\n531\t        .map_err(|_| format!(\"invalid limit number: '{}'\", parts[0]))?;\n532\t    let window_seconds = match parts[1] {\n533\t        \"second\" | \"s\" => 1,\n534\t        \"minute\" | \"m\" => 60,\n535\t        \"hour\" | \"h\" => 3600,\n536\t        \"day\" | \"d\" => 86400,\n537\t        unit => return Err(format!(\"invalid time unit: '{}', expected second/minute/hour/day\", unit)),\n538\t    };\n539\t    Ok((limit, window_seconds))\n540\t}\n541\t\n542\t/// Generate a random session ID.\n543\tfn generate_session_id() -> String {\n544\t    let mut bytes = [0u8; 24];\n545\t    rand::rngs::OsRng.fill_bytes(&mut bytes);\n546\t    hex::encode(&bytes)\n547\t}\n548\t\n549\t/// POST /_miroir/admin/login — admin login with rate limiting and exponential backoff.\n550\t///\n551\t/// Request body:\n552\t/// ```\n560\t///\n561\t/// Rate limiting (per source IP):\n562\t/// - 10 requests per minute (configurable via `admin_ui.rate_limit.per_ip`)\n563\t/// - After 5 consecutive failed attempts, exponential backoff applies:\n564\t///   - 10m, 20m, 40m, ... up to 24h cap\n565\t///\n566\t/// Successful login resets both the rate limit counter and backoff state.\n567\tpub async fn admin_login<S>(\n568\t    State(state): State<S>,\n569\t    headers: HeaderMap,\n570\t    Json(body): Json<AdminLoginRequest>,\n571\t) -> Response\n572\twhere\n573\t    S: Clone + Send + Sync + 'static,\n574\t    AppState: FromRef<S>,\n575\t{\n576\t    let state = AppState::from_ref(&state);\n577\t\n578\t    // Extract source IP from X-Forwarded-For or X-Real-IP (trust proxy)\n579\t    let source_ip = headers\n580\t match redis.check_rate_limit_admin_login(&source_ip, limit, window_seconds) {\n608\t                Ok((allowed, wait_seconds)) => {\n609\t                    if !allowed {\n610\t wait_seconds = ws,\n614\t                                \"admin login rate limited (backoff)\"\n615\t                            );\n616\t                            return (\n617\t  /// - Degraded → Active        (health restored)\n72\t    pub fn transition_to(self, target: NodeStatus) -> Result<NodeStatus> {\n73\t        use NodeStatus::*;\n74\t\n75\t        let legal = match (self, target) {\n76\t            // Normal lifecycle\n77\t            (Joining, Active) => true,\n78\t            (Active, Draining) => true,\n79\t            (Draining, Removed) => true,\n80\t\n81\t Draining) => true,\n99\t\n100\t            // Healthy is an alias for Active in transitions\n101\t            (Healthy, _) | (_, Healthy) => false,\n102\t\n103\t            _ => false,\n104\t        };\n105\t\n106\t        if legal {\n107\t            Ok(target)\n108\t        } else {\n109\t            Err(MiroirError::Topology(format!(\n110\t                \"illegal state transition: {:?} → self.nodes.iter()\n308\t    }\n309\t\n310\t    /// Get a group by ID.\n311\t    pub fn group(&self, id: u32) -> Option<&Group> {\n312\t        self.groups.get(id as usize)\n313\t    }\n314\t\n315\t    /// Iterate over all groups in ascending order by ID.\n316\t    pub fn groups(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Group> {\n317\t        self.groups.iter()\n318\t    }\n319\t\n320\t    /// Get the replication factor.\n321\t    pub fn rf(&self) -> usize {\n322\t        self.rf\n323\t    }\n324\t\n325\t    /// Get the number of replica groups.\n326\t    pub fn replica_group_count(&self) -> u32 {\n327\t        self.groups.len() as u32\n328\t    }\n329\t\n330\t    /// Build a HashMap<NodeId, Node> for use with Group::healthy_nodes.\n331\t    pub fn node_map(&self) -> HashMap<NodeId, Node> {\n332\t        self.nodes.iter().map(|n| (n.id.clone(), n.clone())).collect()\n333\t    }\n334\t\n335\t    fn rebuild_groups(&mut self) {\n336\t        let num_groups = self\n337\t            .nodes\n338\t            .iter()\n339\t            .map(|n| n.replica_group)\n340\t            .max()\n341\t            .map_or(self.replica_groups as usize, |m| (m as usize + 1).max(self.replica_groups as usize));\n342\t\n343\t        self.groups = (0..num_groups).map(|i| Group::new(i as u32)).collect();\n344\t        for node in &self.nodes {\n345\t            if let Some(group) = self.groups.get_mut(node.replica_group as usize) {\n346\t                group.add_node(node.id.clone());\n347\t            }\n348\t        }\n349\t    }\n350\t}\n351\t\n352\timpl Serialize for Topology {\n353\t    fn serialize<S: Serializer>(&self, serializer: S) -> std::result::Result<S::Ok, S::Error> {\n354\t        #[derive(Serialize)]\n355\t        struct TopologyData {\n356\t            shards: u32,\n357\t            replica_groups: u32,\n358\t            rf: usize,\n359\t            nodes: Vec<Node>,\n360\t        }\n361\t        TopologyData {\n362\t            shards: self.shards,\n363\t            replica_groups: self.replica_groups,\n364\t            rf: self.rf,\n365\t            nodes: self.nodes.clone(),\n366\t        }\n367\t        .serialize(serializer)\n368\t    }\n369\t}\n370\t\n371\timpl<'de> Deserialize<'de> for Topology {\n372\t    fn deserialize<D: Deserializer<'de>>(deserializer: D) -> std::result::Result<Self, D::Error> {\n373\t        #[derive(Deserialize)]\n374\t        struct TopologyData {\n375\t            shards: u32,\n376\t            #[serde(default)]\n377\t            replica_groups: u32,\n378\t            #[serde(alias = \"replication_factor\", default)]\n379\t            rf: usize,\n380\t            #[serde(default)]\n381\t            nodes: Vec<Node>,\n382\t        }\n383\t\n384\t        let data = TopologyData::deserialize(deserializer)?;\n385\t        let mut topo = Self {\n386\t            shards: data.shards,\n387\t            replica_groups: data.replica_groups,\n388\t            rf: data.rf,\n389\t            nodes: data.nodes,\n390\t            groups: Vec::new(),\n391\t            node_index: HashMap::new(),\n392\t        };\n393\t        // Build lookup index\n394\t        for (i, node) in topo.nodes.iter().enumerate() {\n395\t            topo.node_index.insert(node.id.clone(), i);\n396\t        }\n397\t        // Derive replica_groups from nodes if not set\n398\t        if topo.replica_groups == 0 && !topo.nodes.is_empty() {\n399\t            topo.replica_groups = topo.nodes.iter().map(|n| n.replica_group).max().unwrap() + 1;\n400\t        }\n401\t        topo.rebuild_groups();\n402\t        Ok(topo)\n403\t    }\n404\t}\n405\t\n406\t#[cfg(test)]\n407\tmod tests {\n408\t    use super::*;\n409\t\n410\t    // ── YAML deserialization {\n526\t        use NodeStatus::*;\n527\t\n528\t        let cases: Vec<(NodeStatus, NodeStatus)> = vec![\n529\t            (Joining, Active),\n530\t            (Active, Draining),\n531\t            (Draining, Removed),\n532\t            (Active, Failed),\n533\t            (Draining, Failed),\n534\t            (Failed, Active),\n535\t            (Active, Degraded),\n536\t            (Failed, Degraded),\n537\t            (Degraded, Active),\n538\t            // Idempotent\n539\t            (Active, Active),\n540\t            (Failed, Failed),\n541\t            (Degraded, Degraded),\n542\t            (Joining, Joining),\n543\t            (Draining, Draining),\n544\t        ];\n545\t\n546\t        for (from, to) in cases {\n547\t            assert!(\n548\t                from.transition_to(to).is_ok(),\n549\t                \"expected {:?} → {:?} to succeed\",\n550\t                from,\n551\t                to\n552\t            );\n553\t        }\n554\t    }\n555\t\n556\t    #[test]\n557\t    fn illegal_transitions() {\n558\t        use NodeStatus::*;\n559\t\n560\t        let cases: Vec<(NodeStatus, NodeStatus)> = vec![\n561\t            // Skip steps\n562\t            (Joining, Draining),\n563\t            (Joining, Failed),\n564\t            (Joining, Removed),\n565\t            (Joining, Degraded),\n566\t            // Can't go back from Draining to Active\n567\t            (Draining, Active),\n568\t            (Draining, Joining),\n569\t            // Can't recover to Joining\n570\t            (Active, Joining),\n571\t            (Failed, Joining),\n572\t            (Degraded, Joining),\n573\t            // Removed is terminal\n574\t            (Removed, Active),\n575\t            (Removed, Joining),\n576\t            (Removed, Failed),\n577\t            (Removed, Degraded),\n578\t            (Removed, Draining),\n579\t            // Healthy not used in transitions\n580\t            (Healthy, Active),\n581\t            (Active, Healthy),\n582\t            // More illegal paths\n583\t            (Failed, Draining),\n584\t            (Failed, Removed),\n585\t            (Degraded, Failed),\n586\t            (Degraded, Draining),\n587\t            (Degraded, Removed),\n588\t        ];\n589\t\n590\t        for (from, to) in cases {\n591\t            let result = from.transition_to(to);\n592\t            assert!(\n593\t                result.is_err(),\n594\t                \"expected {:?} → {:?} to be rejected, but got Ok({:?})\",\n595\t                from,\n596\t                to,\n597\t                result.unwrap()\n598\t            );\n599\t        }\n600\t    }\n601\t\n602\t    #[test]\n603\t    fn node_transition_method() {\n604\t        let mut node = Node::new(\n605\t            NodeId::new(\"n0\".into()),\n606\t            \"http://n0:7700\".into(),\n607\t            0,\n608\t        );\n609\t        assert_eq!(node.status, NodeStatus::Joining);\n610\t\n611\t assert!(node.transition_to(NodeStatus::Joining).is_err());\n616\t        assert_eq!(node.status, NodeStatus::Active); // unchanged\n617\t    }\n618\t\n619\t    #[test]\n620\t    fn provided_origin\n334\t        }\n335\t    } else {\n336\t        provided_origin\n337\t    };\n338\t\n339\t    // Check against allowed origins\n340\t    for allowed in allowed_origins {\n341\t {\n344\t                // Construct origin from scheme (https) and host\n345\t                let same_origin = format!(\"https://{}\", host);\n346\t                if provided_origin == same_origin .join(\"; \")\n420\t}\n421\t\n422\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n423\t// Dispatch verdict\n424\t// Exempt endpoints run their handler directly; rules 1–4\n464\t/// are never consulted.\n465\tpub fn is_dispatch_exempt(method: &Method, path: &str) -> bool {\n466\t    // `GET /health` — unauthenticated liveness probe (Meilisearch-compatible)\n467\t    if method == Method::GET && path == \"/health\" {\n468\t        return true;\n469\t    }\n470\t\n471\t    // `GET /version` —      }\n501\t        }\n502\t    }\n503\t\n504\t    // `GET /ui/search/{index}` — public SPA entry point\n505\t    if method == Method::GET {\n506\t        if let Some(rest) = }\n511\t\n512\t    false\n513\t}\n514\t\n515\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n516\t// Rule 1 — JWT-shape probe\n517\t// timing side-channels on secret key values.\n548\tpub fn constant_time_compare(token: &[u8], expected: &[u8]) -> bool {\n549\t    token.ct_eq(expected).into()\n550\t}\n551\t\n552\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n553\t// Core dispatch — rules 0–4\n554\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n555\t\n556\t/// Execute the full bearer-token dispatch chain for a request.\n557\t///\n558\t/// `bearer_token` is the raw value after stripping `\"Bearer \"` from the\n559\t/// `Authorization` header (may be `None` if the header is absent).\n560\tpub fn dispatch_bearer(\n561\t    method: &Method,\n562\t    path: &str,\n563\t    bearer_token: Option<&str>,\n564\t    state: &AuthState,\n565\t) -> AuthVerdict {\n566\t    // Rule 0 — dispatch-exempt endpoints skip all auth checks\n567\t    if is_dispatch_exempt(method, path) {\n568\t        return AuthVerdict::Exempt;\n569\t    }\n570\t\n571\t    let token = match bearer_token {\n572\t        Some(t) => t,\n573\t        None => return AuthVerdict::InvalidAuth, // Rule 4 — missing auth\n574\t    };\n575\t\n576\t    // Rule 1 — JWT-shape probe, then full validation\n577\t    if probe_jwt_shape(token) {\n578\t        match state.validate_jwt(token) {\n579\t            Ok(_claims) => return AuthVerdict::Authenticated(TokenKind::Jwt),\n580\t            Err(JwtValidationError::PreviousSecretEmpty) => {\n581\t                return AuthVerdict::JwtInvalid;\n582\t            }\n583\t            Err(_) => {\n584\t                return AuthVerdict::JwtInvalid;\n585\t            }\n586\t        }\n587\t    }\n588\t\n589\t    // Rule 2 — admin-path opaque-token match\n590\t    if is_admin_path(path) {\n591\t        if constant_time_compare(token.as_bytes(), state.admin_key.as_bytes()) {\n592\t            return AuthVerdict::Authenticated(TokenKind::AdminKey);\n593\t        }\n594\t        return AuthVerdict::InvalidAuth; // Rule 4\n595\t    }\n596\t\n597\t    // Rule 3 — master-key match (non-admin paths)\n598\t    if constant_time_compare(token.as_bytes(), state.master_key.as_bytes()) {\n599\t        return AuthVerdict::Authenticated(TokenKind::MasterKey);\n600\t    }\n601\t\n602\t    // Rule 4 — mismatch\n603\t    AuthVerdict::InvalidAuth\n604\t}\n605\t\n606\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n607\t// X-Admin-Key short-circuit\n608\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n609\t\n610\t/// Check the `X-Admin-Key` header for admin endpoints.\n611\t/// Returns `true` if the header is present and matches `admin_key`.\n612\t/// Evaluated independently of the bearer chain — short-circuits directly.\n613\tpub fn check_x_admin_key(headers: &HeaderMap, admin_key: &[u8]) -> bool {\n614\t    match headers.get(\"X-Admin-Key\").and_then(|v| v.to_str().ok()) {\n615\t        Some(key) => constant_time_compare(key.as_bytes(), admin_key),\n616\t        None => false,\n617\t    }\n618\t}\n619\t\n620\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n621\t// Axum middleware\n622\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n623\t\n624\t/// Extract the bearer token from `Authorization: Bearer <value>`.\n625\tfn extract_bearer(headers: &HeaderMap) -> Option<&str> {\n626\t    let auth = headers.get(\"authorization\")?.to_str().ok()?;\n627\t    auth.strip_prefix(\"Bearer \")\n628\t}\n629\t\n630\t/// Extract the sealed admin session cookie value from the Cookie header.\n631\tpub fn extract_admin_session_cookie(headers: &HeaderMap) -> Option<String> {\n632\t    let cookie_header = headers.get(\"cookie\")?.to_str().ok()?;\n633\t    for pair in cookie_header.split(';') {\n634\t        let pair = pair.trim();\n635\t        if let Some(value) = pair.strip_prefix(&format!(\"{}=\", admin_session::COOKIE_NAME)) {\n636\t            return Some(value.to_string());\n637\t        }\n638\t    }\n639\t    None\n640\t}\n641\t\n642\t/// Unseal an admin session cookie, returning the session ID.\n643\tpub fn unseal_admin_cookie(cookie_value: &str, key: &SealKey) -> Result<String, admin_session::SealError> {\n644\t    admin_session::unseal_session(cookie_value, key)\n645\t}\n646\t\n647\t/// Axum middleware implementing the bearer-token dispatch chain (plan §5).\n648\tpub async fn auth_middleware(\n649\t    State(state): State<AuthState>,\n650\t    req: Request,\n651\t    next: Next,\n652\t) -> Response {\n653\t    let method = req.method().clone();\n654\t    let path = req.uri().path().to_string();\n655\t\n656\t    // Rule 0 — dispatch-exempt: skip everything, handler decides auth\n657\t    if is_dispatch_exempt(&method, &path) {\n658\t        return next.run(req).await;\n659\t    }\n660\t\n661\t    // X-Admin-Key short-circuit for admin endpoints\n662\t    if is_admin_path(&path) && check_x_admin_key(req.headers(), state.admin_key.as_bytes()) {\n663\t        return next.run(req).await;\n664\t    }\n665\t\n666\t    // Admin session cookie check for admin endpoints (plan §9, §13.19).\n667\t    // If a sealed admin session cookie is present, unseal it and authenticate.\n668\t    // Revoked sessions are rejected immediately.\n669\t    if is_admin_path(&path) {\n670\t        if let Some(cookie_value) = extract_admin_session_cookie(req.headers()) {\n671\t            match unseal_admin_cookie(&cookie_value, &state.seal_key) {\n672\t                Ok(session_id) => {\n673\t                    // Check revocation cache (populated on logout + Pub/Sub).\n674\t                    if state.revoked_sessions.contains_key(&session_id) {\n675\t                        return MeilisearchError::new(\n676\t                            MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n677\t                            \"Admin session has been revoked.\",\n678\t                        )\n679\t                        .into_response();\n680\t                    }\n681\t                    let mut req = req;\n682\t                    req.extensions_mut().insert(AdminSessionId(session_id));\n683\t                    return next.run(req).await;\n684\t                }\n685\t                Err(e) => {\n686\t                    // Cookie tampering or wrong seal key (e.g. cross-pod key\n687\t                    // mismatch in HA).  Log a warning so operators can diagnose\n688\t                    // ADMIN_SESSION_SEAL_KEY divergence across pods.\n689\t                    tracing::warn!(\n690\t                        path = %path,\n691\t                        error = %e,\n692\t                        \"admin session cookie unseal failed — tampered cookie or cross-pod key mismatch\"\n693\t                    );\n694\t                }\n695\t            }\n696\t        }\n697\t    }\n698\t\n699\t    // Extract bearer token\n700\t    let bearer = extract_bearer(req.headers());\n701\t\n702\t    // Run the dispatch chain\n703\t    let verdict = dispatch_bearer(&method, &path, bearer, &state);\n704\t\n705\t    match verdict {\n706\t        AuthVerdict::Authenticated(_) | AuthVerdict::Exempt => next.run(req).await,\n707\t        AuthVerdict::JwtInvalid => MeilisearchError::new(\n708\t            MiroirCode::JwtInvalid,\n709\t            \"The provided JWT is invalid or expired.\",\n710\t        )\n711\t        .into_response(),\n712\t        AuthVerdict::JwtScopeDenied => MeilisearchError::new(\n713\t            MiroirCode::JwtScopeDenied,\n714\t            \"The provided JWT does not grant access to this resource.\",\n715\t        )\n716\t        .into_response(),\n717\t        AuthVerdict::InvalidAuth => MeilisearchError::new(\n718\t            MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n719\t            \"The provided authorization is invalid.\",\n720\t        )\n721\t        .into_response(),\n722\t    }\n723\t}\n724\t\n725\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n726\t// CSRF validation middleware (plan §9)\n727\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n728\t\n729\t/// CSRF middleware that validates `X-CSRF-Token` on state-changing requests.\n730\t///\n731\t/// Bypasses CSRF check when:\n732\t/// - Request is authenticated via Bearer token (not admin session cookie)\n733\t/// - X-Admin-Key header is present\n734\t/// - Request method is safe (GET, HEAD, OPTIONS)\n735\t/// - Path is dispatch-exempt\n736\t///\n737\t/// For admin session cookie auth, requires `X-CSRF-Token` header to match\n738\t/// the token stored in the session.\n739\tpub async fn csrf_middleware(\n740\t    State(state): State<CsrfState>,\n741\t    req: Request,\n742\t    next: Next,\n743\t) -> Response {\n744\t    let method = req.method().clone();\n745\t    let path = req.uri().path().to_string();\n746\t\n747\t    // Skip CSRF for safe methods\n748\t    if matches!(method, Method::GET | Method::HEAD | Method::OPTIONS) {\n749\t        return next.run(req).await;\n750\t    }\n751\t\n752\t    // Skip CSRF for non-admin paths\n753\t    if !is_admin_path(&path) {\n754\t        return next.run(req).await;\n755\t    }\n756\t\n757\t    // Skip CSRF for dispatch-exempt endpoints\n758\t    if is_dispatch_exempt(&method, &path) {\n759\t        return next.run(req).await;\n760\t    }\n761\t\n762\t    // Skip CSRF if X-Admin-Key is present (bypasses CSRF)\n763\t    if check_x_admin_key(req.headers(), state.auth.admin_key.as_bytes()) {\n764\t        return next.run(req).await;\n765\t    }\n766\t\n767\t    // Check if authenticated via admin session cookie\n768\t    let has_session_cookie = extract_admin_session_cookie(req.headers()).is_some();\n769\t    let has_bearer_token = extract_bearer(req.headers()).is_some();\n770\t\n771\t    // CSRF only applies to session-cookie auth, not bearer tokens\n772\t    if !has_session_cookie || has_bearer_token {\n773\t        return next.run(req).await;\n774\t    }\n775\t\n776\t    // Extract CSRF token from header\n777\t    let csrf_token = match extract_csrf_token(req.headers()) {\n778\t        Some(token) => token,\n779\t        None => {\n780\t            return MeilisearchError::new(\n781\t                MiroirCode::MissingCsrf,\n782\t                \"CSRF token is required for state-changing requests.\",\n783\t            )\n784\t            .into_response();\n785\t        }\n786\t    };\n787\t\n788\t    // Get session ID from extensions (set by auth_middleware)\n789\t    let session_id = match req.extensions().get::<AdminSessionId>() {\n790\t        Some(id) => id.0.clone(),\n791\t        None => {\n792\t            // Session cookie was present but auth_middleware didn't set AdminSessionId\n793\t            // This means the session was invalid/expired/revoked\n794\t            return MeilisearchError::new(\n795\t                MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n796\t                \"Admin session is invalid or expired.\",\n797\t            )\n798\t            .into_response();\n799\t        }\n800\t    };\n801\t\n802\t    // Validate CSRF token against session\n803\t    let Some(redis_store) = state.redis_store.as_ref() else {\n804\t        return MeilisearchError::new(\n805\t            MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n806\t            \"Admin sessions require Redis task store.\",\n807\t        )\n808\t        .into_response();\n809\t    };\n810\t\n811\t    let session = match redis_store.get_admin_session(&session_id) {\n812\t        Ok(Some(s)) => s,\n813\t        Ok(None) => {\n814\t            return MeilisearchError::new(\n815\t                MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n816\t                \"Admin session not found.\",\n817\t            )\n818\t            .into_response();\n819\t        }\n820\t        Err(e) => {\n821\t            tracing::warn!(error = %e, session_prefix = &session_id[..session_id.len().min(8)], \"failed to get admin session for CSRF validation\");\n822\t            return MeilisearchError::new(\n823\t                MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n824\t                \"Failed to validate session.\",\n825\t            )\n826\t            .into_response();\n827\t        }\n828\t    };\n829\t\n830\t    // Check if revoked\n831\t    if session.revoked {\n832\t        return MeilisearchError::new(\n833\t            MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n834\t            \"Admin session has been revoked.\",\n835\t        )\n836\t        .into_response();\n837\t    }\n838\t\n839\t    // Check expiration\n840\t    let now = std::time::SystemTime::now()\n841\t        .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)\n842\t        .unwrap_or_default()\n843\t        .as_secs() as i64;\n844\t    if session.expires_at < now {\n845\t        return MeilisearchError::new(\n846\t            MiroirCode::InvalidAuth,\n847\t            \"Admin session has expired.\",\n848\t        )\n849\t        .into_response();\n850\t    }\n851\t\n852\t    // Constant-time compare CSRF tokens\n853\t    if !constant_time_csrf_compare(&csrf_token, &session.csrf_token) {\n854\t        return MeilisearchError::new(\n855\t            MiroirCode::CsrfMismatch,\n856\t            \"CSRF token does not match the session token.\",\n857\t        )\n858\t        .into_response();\n859\t    }\n860\t\n861\t    next.run(req).await\n862\t}\n863\t\n864\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n865\t// Rate-limit hook types (Phase 2 in-memory stub, Phase 6 multi-pod)\n866\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n867\t\n868\t/// Rate-limit bucket key types wired into the dispatch chain.\n869\t/// Phase 2 keeps these as in-memory counters; Phase 6 will back them\n870\t/// with the task store (Redis/SQLite).\n871\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]\n872\tpub enum RateLimitBucket {\n873\t    /// `miroir:ratelimit:adminlogin:<ip>`\n874\t    AdminLogin(String),\n875\t    /// `miroir:ratelimit:searchui:<ip>`\n876\t    SearchUi(String),\n877\t}\n878\t\n879\t/// In-memory rate limiter (Phase 2 stub). Always returns `Ok(())` — actual\n880\t/// enforcement is deferred to Phase 6 multi-pod. The hook is wired here so\n881\t/// handlers can call `limiter.check()` without cfg-gating.\n882\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\n883\tpub struct RateLimiter;\n884\t\n885\timpl RateLimiter {\n886\t    pub fn check(&self, _bucket: &RateLimitBucket) -> Result<(), ()> {\n887\t        Ok(()) // Phase 2: always allow\n888\t    }\n889\t}\n890\t\n891\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n892\t// Helpers\n893\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n894\t\n895\tfn epoch_seconds() -> u64 {\n896\t    std::time::SystemTime::now()\n897\t        .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)\n898\t        .unwrap_or_default()\n899\t        .as_secs()\n900\t}\n901\t\n902\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n903\t// Tests\n904\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n905\t\n906\t#[cfg(test)]\n907\tmod tests {\n908\t    use super::*;\n909\t\n910\t    fn test_key() -> SealKey {\n911\t #[test]\n1636\t    fn constant_time_eq_empty() {\n1637\t        assert!(constant_time_compare(b\"\", b\"\"));\n1638\t    }\n1639\t\n1640\t    /// Timing-injection harness: verify no measurable delta between\n1641\t    /// \"all bytes wrong\" and \"one byte wrong\" comparisons at the same length.\n1642\t    #[test]\n1643\t    fn constant_time_no_timing_leak() {\n1644\t        use std::time::Instant;\n1645\t\n1646\t        let expected = b\"admin-key-456\";\n1647\t        let all_wrong = b\"xxxxxxxxxxxxx\";\n1648\t        let one_wrong = b\"admin-key-457\";\n1649\t\n1650\t        let iterations = 100_000u64;\n1651\t\n1652\t        let start = Instant::now();\n1653\t        for _ in 0..iterations {\n1654\t            let _ = constant_time_compare(all_wrong, expected);\n1655\t        }\n1656\t        let all_wrong_duration = start.elapsed();\n1657\t\n1658\t        let start = Instant::now();\n1659\t        for _ in 0..iterations {\n1660\t            let _ = constant_time_compare(one_wrong, expected);\n1661\t        }\n1662\t        let one_wrong_duration = start.elapsed();\n1663\t\n1664\t        let ratio = all_wrong_duration.as_secs_f64() / one_wrong_duration.as_secs_f64();\n1665\t        assert!(\n1666\t            ratio > 0.5 && ratio < 2.0,\n1667\t            \"Timing ratio {} suggests non-constant-time comparison: all_wrong={:?},    /// Aggregate per-shard preflight responses into global IDF.\n66\t    pub fn from_preflight_responses(responses: &[PreflightResponse]) -> Self {\n67\t        let mut total_docs = 0u64;\n68\t 0.0\n83\t        };\n84\t\n85\t        let n = total_docs as f64;\n86\t        let terms = term_df\n87\t            .into_iter()\n88\t            .map(|(term, df)| {\n89\t                let idf = if ///\n293\t    /// Injects `showRankingScore: true` unconditionally so the merger can global-sort.\n294\t    /// Each node receives `offset + limit` results to ensure the coordinator has enough\n295\t    /// data to apply pagination.\n296\t    pub fn to_node_body(&self) -> Value {\n297\t        let mut body = self.body.clone();\n298\t\n299\t        // Inject showRankingScore: true unconditionally }\n371\t}\n372\t\n373\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(node_count))]\n374\tpub async fn execute_scatter<C: NodeClient>(\n375\t    plan: ScatterPlan,\n376\t    client: &C,\n377\t    req:                                       Err(_) => {\n480\t                                            continue; // Try next replica\n481\t                                        }\n482\t                                    }\n483\t                                }\n484\t                            }\n485\t\n486\t                            if fallback_succeeded {\n487\t                                break; // Found a working replica\n488\t                            }\n489\t                        }\n490\t                    }\n491\t\n492\t                    if !fallback_succeeded {\n493\t                        remaining_failed.insert(shard_id, error.clone());\n494\t                    }\n495\t                }\n496\t\n497\t                // Merge fallback results\n498\t                shard_pages.extend(fallback_pages);\n499\t\n500\t                // Update failed_shards with only those that truly failed\n501\t                if remaining_failed.is_empty() {\n502\t                    // All shards succeeded via fallback\n503\t                    return Ok(ScatterResult {\n504\t                        shard_pages,\n505\t                        failed_shards: HashMap::new(),\n506\t                        partial: false,\n507\t                        deadline_exceeded,\n508\t                    });\n509\t                } else {\n510\t                    // Some shards still failed\n511\t                    failed_shards = remaining_failed;\n512\t                }\n513\t            }\n514\t        }\n515\t    }\n516\t\n517\t    Ok(ScatterResult { shard_pages, failed_shards, partial, deadline_exceeded })\n518\t}\n519\t\n520\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %req.index_uid))]\n521\tpub async fn scatter_gather_search<C: NodeClient>(\n522\t    plan: ScatterPlan,\n523\t    client: &C,\n524\t    req: SearchRequest,\n525\t    topology: &Topology,\n526\t    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n527\t    strategy: &dyn MergeStrategy,\n528\t) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n529\t    let scatter_result = execute_scatter(plan, client, req.clone(), topology, policy).await?;\n530\t\n531\t    let mut shard_pages = scatter_result.shard_pages;\n532\t    if scatter_result.partial {\n533\t        for shard_id in scatter_result.failed_shards.keys() {\n534\t            shard_pages.push(ShardHitPage {\n535\t                body: serde_json::json!({\"success\": false, \"message\": format!(\"shard {} unavailable\", shard_id)}),\n536\t            });\n537\t        }\n538\t    }\n539\t\n540\t    // Collect failed shard IDs for the X-Miroir-Degraded header\n541\t    let failed_shards: Vec<u32> = scatter_result.failed_shards.keys().copied().collect();\n542\t\n543\t    let merge_input = MergeInput {\n544\t        shard_hits: shard_pages,\n545\t        offset: req.offset,\n546\t        limit: req.limit,\n547\t        client_requested_score: req.ranking_score,\n548\t        facets: req.facets.clone(),\n549\t        failed_shards,\n550\t    };\n551\t\n552\t    // Span for the merge operation\n553\t    let _span = info_span!(\n554\t        \"merge\",\n555\t        shard_count = merge_input.shard_hits.len(),\n556\t        offset = req.offset,\n557\t        limit = req.limit,\n558\t    ).entered();\n559\t\n560\t    strategy.merge(merge_input)\n561\t}\n562\t\n563\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n564\t// OP#4: Global-IDF preflight execution\n565\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n566\t\n567\t/// Extract unique query terms from a search query string.\n568\tpub fn extract_query_terms(query: &Option<String>) -> Vec<String> {\n569\t    match query {\n570\t        Some(q) if !q.is_empty() => {\n571\t            let mut seen = std::collections::HashSet::new();\n572\t            let mut terms = Vec::new();\n573\t            for term in q.split_whitespace() {\n574\t                let lower = term.to_lowercase();\n575\t                if seen.insert(lower.clone()) { terms.push(lower); }\n576\t            }\n577\t            terms\n578\t        }\n579\t        _ => Vec::new(),\n580\t    }\n581\t}\n582\t\n583\t/// Execute the preflight phase: gather term frequencies from all shards.\n584\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(node_count, term_count = req.terms.len()))]\n585\tpub async fn execute_preflight<C: NodeClient>(\n586\t    plan: &ScatterPlan,\n587\t    client: &C,\n588\t    req: &PreflightRequest,\n589\t    topology: &Topology,\n590\t) -> Result<GlobalIdf> {\n591\t    if req.terms.is_empty() {\n592\t        return Ok(GlobalIdf { total_docs: 0, avg_doc_length: 0.0, terms: HashMap::new() });\n593\t    }\n594\t\n595\t    let mut node_to_shards: HashMap<NodeId, Vec<u32>> = HashMap::new();\n596\t    for (&shard_id, node_id) in &plan.shard_to_node {\n597\t        if plan.target_shards.contains(&shard_id) {\n598\t            node_to_shards.entry(node_id.clone()).or_default().push(shard_id);\n599\t        }\n600\t    }\n601\t\n602\t    let mut tasks = Vec::new();\n603\t    for (node_id, _) in node_to_shards {\n604\t        let node = match topology.node(&node_id) {\n605\t            Some(n) => n.clone(),\n606\t            None => continue,\n607\t        };\n608\t        let client_ref = client;\n609\t        let req_clone = req.clone();\n610\t        let nid = node_id.clone();\n611\t        tasks.push(async move { client_ref.preflight_node(&nid, &node.address, &req_clone).await });\n612\t    }\n613\t\n614\t    let results = futures_util::future::join_all(tasks).await;\n615\t    let responses: Vec<PreflightResponse> = results.into_iter().filter_map(|r| r.ok()).collect();\n616\t    Ok(GlobalIdf::from_preflight_responses(&responses))\n617\t}\n618\t\n619\t/// Execute a full dfs_query_then_fetch search (OP#4 global-IDF preflight).\n620\t#[instrument(skip_all, fields(index = %req.index_uid))]\n621\tpub async fn dfs_query_then_fetch_search<C: NodeClient>(\n622\t    plan: ScatterPlan,\n623\t    client: &C,\n624\t    req: SearchRequest,\n625\t    topology: &Topology,\n626\t    policy: UnavailableShardPolicy,\n627\t    strategy: &dyn MergeStrategy,\n628\t) -> Result<MergedSearchResult> {\n629\t    let preflight_req = PreflightRequest {\n630\t        index_uid: req.index_uid.clone(),\n631\t        terms: extract_query_terms(&req.query),\n632\t        filter: req.filter.clone(),\n633\t    };\n634\t    let global_idf = execute_preflight(&plan, client, &preflight_req, topology).await?;\n635\t    let mut search_req = req;\n636\t    search_req.global_idf = Some(global_idf);\n637\t    scatter_gather_search(plan, client, search_req, topology, policy, strategy).await\n638\t}\n639\t\n640\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n641\t// Mock client\n642\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n643\t\n644\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]\n645\tpub struct MockNodeClient {\n646\t    pub responses: assert!(!r.degraded);\n917\t        assert!(!r.hits.is_empty());\n918\t    }\n919\t\n920\t    /// Integration test for dfs_query_then_fetch with severely skewed shard distribution.\n921\t    ///\n922\t    /// This test simulates the scenario described in miroir-yio:\n923\t    /// - Shard 0: Normal (1,000 docs, term df = 100)\n924\t    /// - Shard 1: 100x normal (100,000 docs, term df = 10,000)\n925\t    /// - Shard 2: Near-empty (10 docs, term df = 1)\n926\t    ///\n927\t    /// Without global IDF preflight, each shard would compute different local IDF values:\n928\t    /// - Shard 0: IDF ≈ log((1000 - 100 + 0.5) / (100 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n929\t    /// - Shard 1: IDF ≈ log((100000 - 10000 + 0.5) / (10000 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n930\t    /// - Shard 2: IDF ≈ log((10 - 1 + 0.5) / (1 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.8\n931\t    ///\n932\t    /// With global IDF preflight, all shards use the same IDF:\n933\t    /// - Global: N = 101,010, df = 10,101\n934\t    /// - IDF ≈ log((101010 - 10101 + 0.5) / (10101 + 0.5)) + 1 ≈ 2.3\n935\t    ///\n936\t    /// This ensures scores are comparable across shards, enabling correct score-based merge.\n937\t    #[tokio::test]\n938\t    async fn test_dfs_skewed_shards_global_idf_aggregation() {\n939\t        let mut topo = Topology::new(3, 1, 1);\n940\t        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), \"http://node-0:7700\".into(), 0));\n941\t        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), \"http://node-1:7700\".into(), 0));\n942\t        topo.add_node(Node::new(NodeId::new(\"node-2\".into()), \"http://node-2:7700\".into(), 0));\n943\t\n944\t        let plan = plan_search_scatter(&topo, 0, 1, 3);\n945\t\n946\t        // Simulate severely skewed shard distribution\n947\t        let mut c = MockNodeClient::default();\n948\t\n949\t        // Shard 0: Normal distribution\n950\t        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-0\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n951\t            total_docs: 1000,\n952\t            avg_doc_length: 50.0,\n953\t            term_stats: HashMap::from([\n954\t                (\"machine\".into(), TermStats { df: 100 }),\n955\t                (\"learning\".into(), TermStats { df: 80 }),\n956\t            ]),\n957\t        });\n958\t\n959\t        // Shard 1: 100x normal (severely skewed)\n960\t        c.preflight_responses.insert(NodeId::new(\"node-1\".into()), PreflightResponse {\n961\t            total_docs: .iter()\n26\t        .map(|n| (score(shard_id, n.as_str()), n))\n27\t        .collect();\n28\t    scored.sort_unstable_by(|a, b| {\n29\t        b.0.cmp(&a.0)\n30\t            .then_with(|| == 0 {\n52\t        return 0;\n53\t    }\n54\t    (query_seq % replica_groups as u64) as u32\n55\t}\n56\t\n57\t/// The covering set for a search: one node per shard within the chosen group.\n58\tpub as f64;\n517\t\n518\t        // Chi-square statistic: sum((observed - expected)^2 / expected)\n519\t        let chi_square: f64 = counts\n520\t            .iter()\n521\t            .map(|&observed| {\n522\t                let diff = observed as f64 - expected;\n523\t                (diff * diff) / expected\n524\t            })\n525\t            .sum();\n526\t\n527\t        // Degrees of freedom Meilisearch Integration (Search)\n\n**Search handler** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/search.rs`):\n- `POST /search/:index` -- the main search endpoint\n- Implements DFS (Distributed Frequency Search) query-then-fetch pattern:\n  1. **Preflight phase**: Sends term-frequency query to all shards via `execute_preflight()`, aggregates global IDF at coordinator\n  2. **Search phase**: Sends search with global IDF attached so scoring uses corpus-wide statistics\n- Uses `plan_search_scatter()` to build a `ScatterPlan` mapping shards to nodes within a chosen replica group\n- Uses the `NodeClient` trait (implemented by `ProxyNodeClient` wrapping `HttpClient`) for node communication\n- Strips internal fields (`_miroir_shard`, optionally `_rankingScore`) from hits\n- Returns `X-Miroir-Degraded: shards=X,Y,Z` header when shards are unavailable\n- Scoped key integration: checks Redis for a scoped Meilisearch key per index; falls back to `node_master_key` if none exists\n\n**HttpClient** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/client.rs`):\n- Implements `NodeClient` trait for HTTP communication with Meilisearch nodes\n- Methods: `search_node`, `write_documents`, `delete_documents`, `delete_documents_by_filter`, `preflight_node`, `get_task_status`\n- Preflight uses `GET /indexes/{uid}/stats` for total docs and `POST /indexes/{uid}/search` with `limit=0` for term DF\n\n**Scatter module** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/scatter.rs`):\n- `ScatterPlan` -- shard-to-node mapping with chosen group, target shards, hedging eligibility\n- `execute_scatter()` -- fans out requests to all nodes, handles `UnavailableShardPolicy` (partial/error/fallback)\n- `dfs_query_then_fetch_search()` -- full DFS search with global-IDF preflight\n- `MockNodeClient` -- for testing\n\n**Index endpoints** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/indexes.rs`):\n- `POST /indexes` -- creates index on all nodes, auto-adds `_miroir_shard` to filterableAttributes, rollback on failure\n- `DELETE /indexes/:uid` -- broadcast delete to all nodes\n- `GET /indexes/:uid/stats` -- fans out, sums numberOfDocuments (divided by RG*RF for logical count)\n- `PATCH /indexes/:uid/settings/*` -- sequential settings broadcast with rollback (snapshot before apply)\n- `POST /indexes/:uid/_preflight` -- DFS preflight endpoint\n\n**Keys endpoints** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/keys.rs`):\n- `POST /keys` -- create on every node (all-or-nothing with rollback)\n- `PATCH /keys/:key` -- update on every node (sequential with rollback, snapshots pre-change state)\n- `DELETE /keys/:key` -- delete on every node (all-or-nothing)\n- `GET /keys`, `GET /keys/:key` -- proxy to first node\n\n---\n\n### 3. Redis Usage\n\n**Redis TaskStore** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/task_store/redis.rs`):\n- Feature-gated behind `redis-store` (enabled by miroir-proxy)\n- Uses `redis` crate v0.27 with `aio`, `tokio-comp`, `connection-manager`\n- `RedisPool` wraps `ConnectionManager` behind `Arc<Mutex<>>`\n- `RedisTaskStore` has a `key_prefix: \"miroir\"` for all keys\n- Implements the full `TaskStore` trait (14 tables worth of operations)\n\nKey Redis-backed operations:\n- **Task store** (tasks, node_settings_version, aliases, sessions, idempotency_cache, jobs, leader_lease, canaries, canary_runs, cdc_cursors, tenant_map, rollover_policies, search_ui_config, admin_sessions)\n- **Leader lease** (`miroir:lease:{scope}`): `try_acquire_leader_lease()` uses `SET NX EX` with TTL, `renew_leader_lease()` uses `SET XX EX`\n- **Scoped keys** (`miroir:search_ui_scoped_key:{index}`): stores `SearchUiScopedKey` as JSON hash\n- **Pod presence** (`miroir:pod_presence:{pod_id}`): heartbeat with TTL\n- **Observation beacons** (`miroir:search_ui_scoped_key_observed:{pod_id}:{index}`): tracks which pods observed which key generation\n- **Rate limiting**: `check_rate_limit_searchui()`, `check_rate_limit_admin_login()`, `record_failure_admin_login()`, `reset_rate_limit_admin_login()` -- sliding window with exponential backoff\n- **Admin sessions**: CRUD for admin session storage in Redis\n\nRedis is created in `main.rs` if `task_store.backend == \"redis\"`:\n```rust\nlet redis_store = if config.task_store.backend == \"redis\" && !config.task_store.url.is_empty() {\n    Some(RedisTaskStore::open(&url).expect(\"Failed to connect to Redis\"))\n} else {\n    None\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. JWT Signing Secret Rotation** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/auth.rs`):\n- Primary secret (`SEARCH_UI_JWT_SECRET`) signs new tokens; `kid: \"primary\"` identifies it\n- Optional previous secret (`SEARCH_UI_JWT_SECRET_PREVIOUS`) validates old tokens during rotation overlap\n- `sign_jwt()` always signs with primary\n- `validate_jwt()` tries primary first, then previous\n- Full E2E rotation scenario tested: pre-rotation (v1 only) -> during rotation (v2 primary, v1 previous) -> post-rotation (v2 only)\n\n**B. Scoped Meilisearch Key Rotation** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/scoped_key_rotation.rs`):\n- Leader-based rotation sequence (plan 13.21):\n  1. Leader acquires lease via `try_acquire_leader_lease(\"search_ui_key_rotation\", ...)`\n  2. Mints new scoped key via `POST /keys` on all Meilisearch nodes (search-only, index-scoped)\n  3. Writes new generation to Redis hash (`miroir:search_ui_scoped_key:{index}`)\n  4. Waits for all live pods to observe new generation (beacon check via `check_scoped_key_observation()`)\n  5. Drain wait period (configurable `scoped_key_rotation_drain_s`, default 120s)\n  6. Revokes previous key via `DELETE /keys/{previous_uid}` on all nodes\n  7. Clears previous from Redis\n- Background task runs every hour (`run_scoped_key_rotator()`)\n- Manual trigger via `POST /_miroir/ui/search/{index}/rotate-scoped-key` (with optional `force: true`)\n- Timing gate: rotates when `key_age >= (max_age - rotate_before)` (default: rotate 30 days before 60-day max)\n\n**C. Meilisearch API Key Broadcast** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/keys.rs`):\n- All-or-nothing creation with rollback on failure\n- Sequential update with pre-change snapshots and rollback\n- Delete broadcasts to all nodes, tolerates partial failure\n\n**D. Admin Session Cookie Sealing** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/admin_session.rs`):\n- XChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD encryption for session cookies\n- Key loaded from `ADMIN_SESSION_SEAL_KEY` env var (base64-encoded 32 bytes) or generated randomly\n- Wire format: `[24-byte XNonce][ciphertext + 16-byte Poly1305 tag]` base64-encoded\n- Cross-pod key mismatch detected and warned about\n\n**E. Search Key Selection** (in search handler):\n- Search requests use scoped key from Redis if available (primary_key, with previous_key as overlap fallback)\n- Falls back to `node_master_key` for initial setup or single-pod dev mode\n- Each search refreshes the pod's observation beacon\n\n---\n\n### 6. Meilisearch Integration (Search)\n\n**Search handler** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/search.rs`):\n- `POST /search/:index` -- the main search endpoint\n- Implements DFS (Distributed Frequency Search) query-then-fetch pattern:\n  1. **Preflight phase**: Sends term-frequency query to all shards via `execute_preflight()`, aggregates global IDF at coordinator\n  2. **Search phase**: Sends search with global IDF attached so scoring uses corpus-wide statistics\n- Uses `plan_search_scatter()` to build a `ScatterPlan` mapping shards to nodes within a chosen replica group\n- Uses the `NodeClient` trait (implemented by `ProxyNodeClient` wrapping `HttpClient`) for node communication\n- Strips internal fields (`_miroir_shard`, optionally `_rankingScore`) from hits\n- Returns `X-Miroir-Degraded: shards=X,Y,Z` header when shards are unavailable\n- Scoped key integration: checks Redis for a scoped Meilisearch key per index; falls back to `node_master_key` if none exists\n\n**HttpClient** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/client.rs`):\n- Implements `NodeClient` trait for HTTP communication with Meilisearch nodes\n- Methods: `search_node`, `write_documents`, `delete_documents`, `delete_documents_by_filter`, `preflight_node`, `get_task_status`\n- Preflight uses `GET /indexes/{uid}/stats` for total docs and `POST /indexes/{uid}/search` with `limit=0` for term DF\n\n**Scatter module** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/scatter.rs`):\n- `ScatterPlan` -- shard-to-node mapping with chosen group, target shards, hedging eligibility\n- `execute_scatter()` -- fans out requests to all nodes, handles `UnavailableShardPolicy` (partial/error/fallback)\n- `dfs_query_then_fetch_search()` -- full DFS search with global-IDF preflight\n- `MockNodeClient` -- for testing\n\n**Index endpoints** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/indexes.rs`):\n- `POST /indexes` -- creates index on all nodes, auto-adds `_miroir_shard` to filterableAttributes, rollback on failure\n- `DELETE /indexes/:uid` -- broadcast delete to all nodes\n- `GET /indexes/:uid/stats` -- fans out, sums numberOfDocuments (divided by RG*RF for logical count)\n- `PATCH /indexes/:uid/settings/*` -- sequential settings broadcast with rollback (snapshot before apply)\n- `POST /indexes/:uid/_preflight` -- DFS preflight endpoint\n\n**Keys endpoints** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/keys.rs`):\n- `POST /keys` -- create on every node (all-or-nothing with rollback)\n- `PATCH /keys/:key` -- update on every node (sequential with rollback, snapshots pre-change state)\n- `DELETE /keys/:key` -- delete on every node (all-or-nothing)\n- `GET /keys`, `GET /keys/:key` -- proxy to first node\n\n---\n\n### 3. Redis Usage\n\n**Redis TaskStore** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-core/src/task_store/redis.rs`):\n- Feature-gated behind `redis-store` (enabled by miroir-proxy)\n- Uses `redis` crate v0.27 with `aio`, `tokio-comp`, `connection-manager`\n- `RedisPool` wraps `ConnectionManager` behind `Arc<Mutex<>>`\n- `RedisTaskStore` has a `key_prefix: \"miroir\"` for all keys\n- Implements the full `TaskStore` trait (14 tables worth of operations)\n\nKey Redis-backed operations:\n- **Task store** (tasks, node_settings_version, aliases, sessions, idempotency_cache, jobs, leader_lease, canaries, canary_runs, cdc_cursors, tenant_map, rollover_policies, search_ui_config, admin_sessions)\n- **Leader lease** (`miroir:lease:{scope}`): `try_acquire_leader_lease()` uses `SET NX EX` with TTL, `renew_leader_lease()` uses `SET XX EX`\n- **Scoped keys** (`miroir:search_ui_scoped_key:{index}`): stores `SearchUiScopedKey` as JSON hash\n- **Pod presence** (`miroir:pod_presence:{pod_id}`): heartbeat with TTL\n- **Observation beacons** (`miroir:search_ui_scoped_key_observed:{pod_id}:{index}`): tracks which pods observed which key generation\n- **Rate limiting**: `check_rate_limit_searchui()`, `check_rate_limit_admin_login()`, `record_failure_admin_login()`, `reset_rate_limit_admin_login()` -- sliding window with exponential backoff\n- **Admin sessions**: CRUD for admin session storage in Redis\n\nRedis is created in `main.rs` if `task_store.backend == \"redis\"`:\n```rust\nlet redis_store = if config.task_store.backend == \"redis\" && !config.task_store.url.is_empty() {\n    Some(RedisTaskStore::open(&url).expect(\"Failed to connect to Redis\"))\n} else {\n    None\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. Proxy/Admin Routes\n\n**Route structure** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/mod.rs`):\n```\nadmin, admin_endpoints, documents, health, indexes, keys, search, session, settings, tasks, version\n```\n\n**Router setup** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/main.rs`):\n```rust\n.route(\"/health\", get(health::get_health))\n.route(\"/version\", get(version::get_version))\n.route(\"/stats\", get(indexes::global_stats_handler))\n.nest(\"/_miroir\", admin::router::<UnifiedState>())     // Admin surface\n.nest(\"/indexes\", indexes::router::<UnifiedState>())    // Index CRUD + settings\n.nest(\"/keys\", keys::router::<UnifiedState>())          // Key management\n.nest(\"/search\", search::router::<UnifiedState>())      // Search\n.nest(\"/settings\", settings::router::<UnifiedState>())  // Settings\n.nest(\"/tasks\", tasks::router::<UnifiedState>())        // Tasks\n```\n\n**Admin router** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/admin.rs`):\n```\nPOST /_miroir/admin/login        -- admin login (dispatch-exempt)\nGET  /_miroir/admin/session       -- validate session\nPOST /_miroir/admin/logout       -- revoke session\nGET  /_miroir/ui/search/{index}/session  -- search UI JWT session\nGET  /_miroir/topology           -- cluster topology\nGET  /_miroir/shards             -- shard-to-node mapping\nGET  /_miroir/ready              -- readiness probe\nGET  /_miroir/metrics            -- admin-gated Prometheus metrics\nPOST /_miroir/ui/search/{index}/rotate-scoped-key  -- manual key rotation\n```\n\n**Middleware layers** (applied in order, bottom-up):\n1. `telemetry_middleware` -- request IDs, timing, metrics\n2. `csrf_middleware` -- CSRF validation for state-changing admin requests with session cookies\n3. `auth_middleware` -- bearer token dispatch chain (rules 0-4)\n4. `DefaultBodyLimit` -- 100 MiB max\n5. Config extension\n6. AppState extension\n7. `request_id_middleware` -- X-Request-ID generation/passthrough\n\n---\n\n### 5. Key Management and Rotation\n\n**A. JWT Signing Secret Rotation** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/auth.rs`):\n- Primary secret (`SEARCH_UI_JWT_SECRET`) signs new tokens; `kid: \"primary\"` identifies it\n- Optional previous secret (`SEARCH_UI_JWT_SECRET_PREVIOUS`) validates old tokens during rotation overlap\n- `sign_jwt()` always signs with primary\n- `validate_jwt()` tries primary first, then previous\n- Full E2E rotation scenario tested: pre-rotation (v1 only) -> during rotation (v2 primary, v1 previous) -> post-rotation (v2 only)\n\n**B. Scoped Meilisearch Key Rotation** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/scoped_key_rotation.rs`):\n- Leader-based rotation sequence (plan 13.21):\n  1. Leader acquires lease via `try_acquire_leader_lease(\"search_ui_key_rotation\", ...)`\n  2. Mints new scoped key via `POST /keys` on all Meilisearch nodes (search-only, index-scoped)\n  3. Writes new generation to Redis hash (`miroir:search_ui_scoped_key:{index}`)\n  4. Waits for all live pods to observe new generation (beacon check via `check_scoped_key_observation()`)\n  5. Drain wait period (configurable `scoped_key_rotation_drain_s`, default 120s)\n  6. Revokes previous key via `DELETE /keys/{previous_uid}` on all nodes\n  7. Clears previous from Redis\n- Background task runs every hour (`run_scoped_key_rotator()`)\n- Manual trigger via `POST /_miroir/ui/search/{index}/rotate-scoped-key` (with optional `force: true`)\n- Timing gate: rotates when `key_age >= (max_age - rotate_before)` (default: rotate 30 days before 60-day max)\n\n**C. Meilisearch API Key Broadcast** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/routes/keys.rs`):\n- All-or-nothing creation with rollback on failure\n- Sequential update with pre-change snapshots and rollback\n- Delete broadcasts to all nodes, tolerates partial failure\n\n**D. Admin Session Cookie Sealing** (`/home/coding/miroir/crates/miroir-proxy/src/admin_session.rs`):\n- XChaCha20-Poly1305 AEAD encryption for session cookies\n- Key loaded from `ADMIN_SESSION_SEAL_KEY` env var (base64-encoded 32 bytes) or generated randomly\n- Wire format: `[24-byte XNonce][ciphertext + 16-byte Poly1305 tag]` base64-encoded\n- Cross-pod key mismatch detected and warned about\n\n**E. Search Key Selection** (in search handler):\n- Search requests use scoped key from Redis if available (primary_key, with previous_key as overlap fallback)\n- Falls back to `node_master_key` for initial setup or single-pod dev mode\n- Each search refreshes the pod's observation beacon\n\n---\n\n### 6. endpoint.\n#[derive(serde::Serialize)]\npub struct RotateScopedKeyResponse {\n    pub status: String,\n    pub index_uid: String,\n    pub generation: i64,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub previous_uid_revoked: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pub error: Option<String>,\n}\n\n/// Request body for the manual rotation endpoint.\n#[derive(serde::Deserialize)]\npub struct RotateScopedKeyRequest {\n    /// If true, bypass the timing gate and rotate immediately.\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub force: bool,\n}\n\n/// Run the background scoped key rotation loop.\npub async fn run_scoped_key_rotator(state: ScopedKeyRotationState) {\n    if !state.config.search_ui.enabled {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    let check_interval = Duration::from_secs(3600); // Check every hour\n    let mut interval = tokio::time::interval(check_interval);\n\n    info!(\"scoped key rotation background task started\");\n\n    loop {\n        interval.tick().await;\n\n        // Refresh our own pod presence heartbeat\n        if let Err(e) = state.redis.register_pod_presence(&state.pod_id) {\n            warn!(pod_id = %state.pod_id, error = %e, \"failed to register pod presence\");\n        }\n\n        // Try to acquire the rotation leader lease\n        let lease_scope = \"search_ui_key_rotation\";\n        let lease_now = now_ms();\n        let lease_ttl_ms = (state.config.leader_election.lease_ttl_s as i64) * 1000;\n        let expires_at = lease_now + lease_ttl_ms;\n\n        match state.redis.try_acquire_leader_lease(lease_scope, &state.pod_id, expires_at, lease_now) {\n            Ok(true) => {}\n            Ok(false) => continue, // Another pod holds the lease\n            Err(e) => {\n                warn!(error = %e, \"failed to acquire rotation leader lease\");\n                continue;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // We are the leader — check each index for rotation need\n        let indexes = discover_scoped_indexes(&state).await;\n        for index_uid in indexes {\n            if let Err(e) = check_and_rotate(&state, &index_uid, false).await {\n                error!(index = %index_uid, error = %e, \"scoped key rotation failed\");\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Renew the lease\n        let _ = state.redis.renew_leader_lease(\n            lease_scope,\n            &state.pod_id,\n            now_ms() + lease_ttl_ms,\n        );\n    }\n}\n\n/// Check if a scoped key needs rotation and perform it if so.\npub async fn check_and_rotate(\n    state: &ScopedKeyRotationState,\n    index_uid: &str,\n    force: bool,\n) -> Result<RotateScopedKeyResponse, String> {\n    let current = state.redis.get_search_ui_scoped_key(index_uid)\n        .map_err(|e| format!(\"redis read failed: {e}\"))?;\n\n    // Timing gate check (skip if force)\n    if !force {\n        if !should_rotate(&current, &state.config) {\n            return Ok(RotateScopedKeyResponse {\n                status: \"skipped\".into(),\n                index_uid: index_uid.into(),\n                generation: current.as_ref().map(|k| k.generation).unwrap_or(0),\n                previous_uid_revoked: None,\n                error: None,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Step 1: Mint new scoped key via Meilisearch POST /keys\n    let client = MeilisearchClient::new(state.config.node_master_key.clone());\n    let (new_key, new_uid) = mint_scoped_key(&client, &state.config, index_uid).await?;\n\n    // Step 2: Write new generation to Redis\n    let new_generation = current.as_ref().map(|k| k.generation + 1).unwrap_or(1);\n    let previous_uid = current.as_ref().map(|k| k.primary_uid.clone());\n    let previous_key = current.as_ref().map(|k| k.primary_key.clone());\n\n    let scoped_key = SearchUiScopedKey {\n        index_uid: index_uid.into(),\n        primary_key: new_key.clone(),\n        primary_uid: new_uid.clone(),\n        previous_key,\n        previous_uid: previous_uid.clone(),\n        rotated_at: now_ms(),\n        generation: new_generation,\n    };\n\n    state.redis.set_search_ui_scoped_key(&scoped_key)\n        .map_err(|e| format!(\"redis write failed: {e}\"))?;\n\n    info!(\n        index = %index_uid,\n        generation = new_generation,\n        \"new scoped key minted, waiting for pod observation\"\n    );\n\n    // Step 3: Observe our own beacon immediately\n    state.redis.observe_search_ui_scoped_key(\n        &state.pod_id,\n        index_uid,\n        new_generation,\n    ).map_err(|e| format!(\"beacon write failed: {e}\"))?;\n\n    // Step 4: Wait for drain period and check beacons\n    let drain_s = state.config.search_ui.scoped_key_rotation_drain_s;\n    let drain_deadline = tokio::time::Instant::now() + Duration::from_secs(drain_s);\n\n    let mut previous_revoked: Option<String> = None;\n\n    loop {\n        // Get live pods\n        let live_pods = state.redis.get_live_pods()\n            .map_err(|e| format!(\"get_live_pods failed: {e}\"))?;\n\n        // Check if all live pods have observed the new generation\n        let (all_observed, unobserved) = state.redis.check_scoped_key_observation(\n            index_uid,\n            new_generation,\n            &live_pods,\n        ).map_err(|e| format!(\"beacon check failed: {e}\"))?;\n\n        if all_observed {\n            info!(\n                index = %index_uid,\n                generation = new_generation,\n                \"all live pods observed new generation, revoking previous key\"\n            );\n\n            // Step 6: Delete previous key from Meilisearch and clear from Redis\n            if let Some(ref prev_uid) = previous_uid {\n                if let Err(e) = revoke_previous_key(&client, &state.config, prev_uid).await {\n                    warn!(previous_uid = %prev_uid, error = %e, \"failed to revoke previous key, will retry\");\n                } else {\n                    previous_revoked = Some(prev_uid.clone());\n                    // Clear previous from Redis\n                    if let Err(e) = state.redis.clear_scoped_key_previous(index_uid) {\n                        warn!(error = %e, \"failed to clear previous key from redis\");\n                    }\n                    info!(index = %index_uid, previous_uid = %prev_uid, \"previous scoped key revoked\");\n                }\n            }\n\n            return Ok(RotateScopedKeyResponse {\n                status: \"rotated\".into(),\n                index_uid: index_uid.into(),\n                generation: new_generation,\n                previous_uid_revoked: previous_revoked,\n                error: None,\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Not all pods have caught up yet\n        if tokio::time::Instant::now() >= drain_deadline {\n            warn!(\n                index = %index_uid,\n unobserved.len()\n            );\n\n            return Ok(RotateScopedKeyResponse {\n                status: \"drain_pending\".into(),\n                index_uid: index_uid.into(),\n unobserved.len(),\n                    unobserved.join(\", \")\n                )),\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Wait before rechecking (every 10 seconds)\n fn mint_scoped_key(\n    client: &MeilisearchClient,\n    config: &MiroirConfig,\n    index_uid: &str,\n) -> Result<(String, String), String> {\n    let description = format!(\"miroir search-ui scoped {\n82\t        // Check cache first\n83\t        {\n84\t            let cache = self.version_cache.read().await;\n85\t            let last_update = self.last_cache_update.read().await;\n86\t            if let (Some(ref cached), Some(last)) = (cache.as_ref(), last_update.as_ref()) {\n87\t                if last.elapsed().as_secs() < self.cache_ttl_secs {\n88\t                    return Ok((**cached).clone());\n89\t                }\n90\t            }\n91\t        }\n92\t\n93\t        // Cache miss or expired - fetch from a node\n94\t        let client = Client::builder()\n95\t            .timeout(Duration::from_secs(2))\n96\t            .build()\n97\t            .map_err(|_| StatusCode::INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)?;\n98\t\n99\t        for address in &self.node_addresses {\n100\t format!(\"Bearer {}\", self.node_master_key))\n104\t                .send()\n105\t                .await;\n106\t\n107\t            if let Ok(resp) = response {\n108\t                if resp.status().is_success() {\n109\t                    if let Ok(body) = resp.text().await {\n110\t                        // Update cache\n111\t                        *self.version_cache.write().await = Some(body.clone());\n112\t                        *self.last_cache_update.write().await = Some(std::time::Instant::now());\n113\t                        return ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n124\t// Local Rate Limiter (for single-pod deployments)\n125\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n126\t\n127\t/// In-memory rate limiter for admin login (local backend only).\n128\t/// Thread-safe using Arc<Mutex<...>>.\n129\t#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\n130\tpub struct LocalAdminRateLimiter {\n131\t    inner: Arc<std::sync::Mutex<LocalAdminRateLimiterInner>>,\n132\t}\n133\t\n134\t#[derive(Debug, Default)]\n135\tstruct LocalAdminRateLimiterInner {\n136\t    /// Map of IP -> (request_timestamps_ms, failed_count, backoff_until_ms)\n137\t    state: HashMap<String, LocalRateLimitState>,\n138\t}\n139\t\n140\t#[derive(Debug, Default, Clone)]\n141\tstruct LocalRateLimitState {\n142\t    /// Timestamps of recent requests (for sliding window)\n143\t    request_timestamps_ms: Vec<i64>,\n144\t    /// Consecutive failed login attempts\n145\t    failed_count: u32,\n146\t    /// Unix timestamp (ms) when backoff expires\n147\t    backoff_until_ms: Option<i64>,\n148\t}\n149\t\n150\timpl LocalAdminRateLimiter {\n151\t    pub fn new() -> Self {\n152\t        Self {\n153\t            inner: Arc::new(std::sync::Mutex::new(LocalAdminRateLimiterInner::default())),\n154\t        }\n155\t    }\n156\t\n157\t    /// Check rate limit and exponential backoff.\n158\t    /// Returns (allowed, wait_seconds).\n159\t    pub fn check(\n160\t        &self,\n161\t        ip: &str,\n162\t        limit: u64,\n163\t        window_ms: u64,\n164\t        failed_threshold: u32,\n165\t        backoff_start_minutes: u64,\n166\t        backoff_max_hours: u64,\n167\t    ) -> (bool, Option<u64>) {\n168\t        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n169\t        let now = now_ms();\n170\t        let state = inner.state.entry(ip.to_string()).or_default();\n171\t\n172\t        // Check if we're in backoff mode\n173\t        if let Some(backoff_until) = state.backoff_until_ms {\n174\t            if backoff_until > now {\n175\t                let wait_seconds = ((backoff_until - now) / 1000) as u64;\n176\t                return (false, Some(wait_seconds));\n177\t            }\n178\t            // Backoff expired, clear it\n179\t            state.backoff_until_ms = None;\n180\t        }\n181\t\n182\t        // Clean old timestamps outside the window\n183\t        state.request_timestamps_ms.retain(|&ts| now - ts < window_ms as i64);\n184\t\n185\t        // Check if limit exceeded\n186\t        if state.request_timestamps_ms.len() >= limit as usize {\n187\t            // Enter backoff mode after threshold consecutive failures\n188\t            let failed = state.failed_count + 1;\n189\t            state.failed_count = failed;\n190\t\n191\t            if failed >= failed_threshold {\n192\t                let backoff_minutes = backoff_start_minutes * (1u64 << ((failed - failed_threshold) as u64).min(7)); // Cap at 2^7 = 128x\n193\t                let backoff_seconds = (backoff_minutes * 60).min(backoff_max_hours * 3600);\n194\t                state.backoff_until_ms = Some(now + (backoff_seconds as i64 * 1000));\n195\t                return (false, Some(backoff_seconds));\n196\t            }\n197\t\n198\t            return (false, None);\n199\t        }\n200\t\n201\t        // Record this request\n202\t        state.request_timestamps_ms.push(now);\n203\t        (true, None)\n204\t    }\n205\t\n206\t    /// Reset rate limit and backoff state on successful login.\n207\t    pub fn reset(&self, ip: &str) {\n208\t        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n209\t        inner.state.remove(ip);\n210\t    }\n211\t\n212\t    /// Record a failed login attempt (for backoff calculation).\n213\t    pub fn record_failure(&self, ip: &str, failed_threshold: u32, backoff_start_minutes: u64, backoff_max_hours: u64) -> Option<u64> {\n214\t        let mut inner = self.inner.lock().unwrap();\n215\t        let now = now_ms();\n216\t        let state = inner.state.entry(ip.to_string()).or_default();\n217\t\n218\t        state.failed_count += 1;\n219\t\n220\t        if state.failed_count >= failed_threshold {\n221\t            let backoff_minutes = backoff_start_minutes * (1u64 << ((state.failed_count - failed_threshold) as u64).min(7));\n222\t            let backoff_seconds = (backoff_minutes * 60).min(backoff_max_hours * 3600);\n223\t            state.backoff_until_ms = Some(now + (backoff_seconds as i64 * 1000));\n224\t            return Some(backoff_seconds);\n225\t        }\n226\t\n227\t        None\n228\t    }\n229\t}\n230\t\n231\timpl Default for LocalAdminRateLimiter {\n232\t    fn default() -> Self {\n233\t        Self::new()\n234\t    }\n235\t}\n236\t\n237\t/// Get current time in milliseconds since Unix epoch.\n238\tfn now_ms() -> i64 {\n239\t    std::time::SystemTime::now()\n240\t        .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)\n241\t        .unwrap_or_default()\n242\t        .as_millis() as i64\n243\t}\n244\t\n245\t/// Shared application state for admin }\n334\t}\n335\t\n336\t/// Response for GET /_miroir/topology (plan §10 JSON shape).\n337\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n338\tpub struct TopologyResponse {\n339\t    pub shards:
